# GIK.NAME : Name of the City Electoral Committee [text];
# TIK.NAME : Name of the Territorial Electoral Committee [text];
# UIK.NAME : Name of the Polling Station Electoral Committee [text];
# MO.NAME : Name of the Municipality [text];
# MO.DISTRICT : Municipal District [text];
# LAT.ik : Polling station office location: Latitude [numeric];
# LON.ik : Polling station office location: Longitude [numeric];
# LAT.voteroom : Polling station vote room location: Latitude [numeric];
# LON.voteroom : Polling station vote room location: Longitude [numeric];
# UIK.NAME.short : Name of the Polling Station Electoral Committee, abbreviated [text];
# TIK : Territorial Electoral Committee Numeric Code [integer];
# UIK : Polling station Numeric Code [integer];
# VOTERS : Number of woters registered with the Poling Station [integer];
# BALL.RECEIVED : Number of blank ballots received [integer];
# BALL.ISS.UIK.DAYOFVOTE : Number of blank ballots issued at the polling station on the day of vote [integer];
# BALL.ISS.EXTRA : Number of blank ballots issued outside the polling station on the day of vote [integer];
# BALL.CANCELLED : Number of blank ballots cancelled [integer];
# BALL.PORTABLE_BOXES : Number of ballots found in the portable ballot boxes [integer];
# BALL.STATIONARY_BOXES : Number of ballots found in the stationary ballot boxes [integer];
# BALL.INVALID : Number of invalid ballots cast [integer];
# BALL.VALID : Number of valid ballots cast [integer];
# BALL.LOST : Number of ballots lost [integer];
# BALL.NOT.RECORDED : Number of blank ballots received by the polling station from the Territorial Electoral Commission but not reported in BULL.RECEIVED [integer];
# AMOSOV : Number of ballots cast for Mikhail Amosov [integer];
# BEGLOV : Number of ballots cast for Alexander Beglov [integer];
# TIKHONOVA : Number of ballots cast for Nadezhda Tikhonova [integer];
